11. EDIT /workspace/raft/storage.go
Before
// ApplySnapshot overwrites the contents of this Storage object with
// those of the given snapshot.
func (ms *MemoryStorage) ApplySnapshot(snap pb.Snapshot) error {
	ms.Lock()
	defer ms.Unlock()

	//handle check for old snapshot being applied
	msIndex := ms.snapshot.Metadata.Index
	snapIndex := snap.Metadata.Index
	// During bootstrap, applications (e.g., etcd) may initialize only the
	// ConfState in the snapshot. In this case, both the snapshot index and
	// term are 0.
	if msIndex != 0 && msIndex >= snapIndex {
		return ErrSnapOutOfDate
	}

	ms.snapshot = snap
	ms.ents = []pb.Entry{{Term: snap.Metadata.Term, Index: snap.Metadata.Index}}
	return nil
}
After
// ApplySnapshot overwrites the contents of this Storage object with
// those of the given snapshot.
func (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) ApplySnapshot(snap pb.Snapshot) error {
	ms.Lock()
	defer ms.Unlock()

	//handle check for old snapshot being applied
	msIndex := ms.snapshot.Metadata.Index
	snapIndex := snap.Metadata.Index
	// During bootstrap, applications (e.g., etcd) may initialize only the
	// ConfState in the snapshot. In this case, both the snapshot index and
	// term are 0.
	if msIndex != 0 && msIndex >= snapIndex {
		return ErrSnapOutOfDate
	}

	ms.snapshot = snap
	ms.ents = []pb.Entry{{Term: snap.Metadata.Term, Index: snap.Metadata.Index}}
	return nil
}
12. EDIT /workspace/raft/storage.go
Before
// CreateSnapshot makes a snapshot which can be retrieved with Snapshot() and
// can be used to reconstruct the state at that point.
// If any configuration changes have been made since the last compaction,
// the result of the last ApplyConfChange must be passed in.
func (ms *MemoryStorage) CreateSnapshot(i uint64, cs *pb.ConfState, data []byte) (pb.Snapshot, error) {
	ms.Lock()
	defer ms.Unlock()
	if i <= ms.snapshot.Metadata.Index {
		return pb.Snapshot{}, ErrSnapOutOfDate
	}

	offset := ms.ents[0].Index
	if i > ms.lastIndex() {
		getLogger().Panicf("snapshot %d is out of bound lastindex(%d)", i, ms.lastIndex())
	}

	ms.snapshot.Metadata.Index = i
	ms.snapshot.Metadata.Term = ms.ents[i-offset].Term
	if cs != nil {
		ms.snapshot.Metadata.ConfState = *cs
	}
	ms.snapshot.Data = data
	return ms.snapshot, nil
}
After
// CreateSnapshot makes a snapshot which can be retrieved with Snapshot() and
// can be used to reconstruct the state at that point.
// If any configuration changes have been made since the last compaction,
// the result of the last ApplyConfChange must be passed in.
func (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) CreateSnapshot(i uint64, cs *pb.ConfState, data []byte) (pb.Snapshot, error) {
	ms.Lock()
	defer ms.Unlock()
	if i <= ms.snapshot.Metadata.Index {
		return pb.Snapshot{}, ErrSnapOutOfDate
	}

	offset := ms.ents[0].Index
	if i > ms.lastIndex() {
		getLogger().Panicf("snapshot %d is out of bound lastindex(%d)", i, ms.lastIndex())
	}

	ms.snapshot.Metadata.Index = i
	ms.snapshot.Metadata.Term = ms.ents[i-offset].Term
	if cs != nil {
		ms.snapshot.Metadata.ConfState = *cs
	}
	ms.snapshot.Data = data
	return ms.snapshot, nil
}
13. EDIT /workspace/raft/storage.go
Before
// Compact discards all log entries prior to compactIndex.
// It is the application's responsibility to not attempt to compact an index
// greater than raftLog.applied.
func (ms *MemoryStorage) Compact(compactIndex uint64) error {
	ms.Lock()
	defer ms.Unlock()
	offset := ms.ents[0].Index
	if compactIndex <= offset {
		return ErrCompacted
	}
	if compactIndex > ms.lastIndex() {
		getLogger().Panicf("compact %d is out of bound lastindex(%d)", compactIndex, ms.lastIndex())
	}

	i := compactIndex - offset
	// NB: allocate a new slice instead of reusing the old ms.ents. Entries in
	// ms.ents are immutable, and can be referenced from outside MemoryStorage
	// through slices returned by ms.Entries().
	ents := make([]pb.Entry, 1, uint64(len(ms.ents))-i)
	ents[0].Index = ms.ents[i].Index
	ents[0].Term = ms.ents[i].Term
	ents = append(ents, ms.ents[i+1:]...)
	ms.ents = ents
	return nil
}
After
// Compact discards all log entries prior to compactIndex.
// It is the application's responsibility to not attempt to compact an index
// greater than raftLog.applied.
func (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) Compact(compactIndex uint64) error {
	ms.Lock()
	defer ms.Unlock()
	offset := ms.ents[0].Index
	if compactIndex <= offset {
		return ErrCompacted
	}
	if compactIndex > ms.lastIndex() {
		getLogger().Panicf("compact %d is out of bound lastindex(%d)", compactIndex, ms.lastIndex())
	}

	i := compactIndex - offset
	// NB: allocate a new slice instead of reusing the old ms.ents. Entries in
	// ms.ents are immutable, and can be referenced from outside InMemoryRaftLog
	// through slices returned by ms.Entries().
	ents := make([]pb.Entry, 1, uint64(len(ms.ents))-i)
	ents[0].Index = ms.ents[i].Index
	ents[0].Term = ms.ents[i].Term
	ents = append(ents, ms.ents[i+1:]...)
	ms.ents = ents
	return nil
}
14. EDIT /workspace/raft/storage.go
Before
// Append the new entries to storage.
// TODO (xiangli): ensure the entries are continuous and
// entries[0].Index > ms.entries[0].Index
func (ms *MemoryStorage) Append(entries []pb.Entry) error {
	if len(entries) == 0 {
		return nil
	}

	ms.Lock()
	defer ms.Unlock()

	first := ms.firstIndex()
	last := entries[0].Index + uint64(len(entries)) - 1

	// shortcut if there is no new entry.
	if last < first {
		return nil
	}
	// truncate compacted entries
	if first > entries[0].Index {
		entries = entries[first-entries[0].Index:]
	}

	offset := entries[0].Index - ms.ents[0].Index
	switch {
	case uint64(len(ms.ents)) > offset:
		// NB: full slice expression protects ms.ents at index >= offset from
		// rewrites, as they may still be referenced from outside MemoryStorage.
		ms.ents = append(ms.ents[:offset:offset], entries...)
	case uint64(len(ms.ents)) == offset:
		ms.ents = append(ms.ents, entries...)
	default:
		getLogger().Panicf("missing log entry [last: %d, append at: %d]",
			ms.lastIndex(), entries[0].Index)
	}
	return nil
}
After
// Append the new entries to storage.
// TODO (xiangli): ensure the entries are continuous and
// entries[0].Index > ms.entries[0].Index
func (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) Append(entries []pb.Entry) error {
	if len(entries) == 0 {
		return nil
	}

	ms.Lock()
	defer ms.Unlock()

	first := ms.firstIndex()
	last := entries[0].Index + uint64(len(entries)) - 1

	// shortcut if there is no new entry.
	if last < first {
		return nil
	}
	// truncate compacted entries
	if first > entries[0].Index {
		entries = entries[first-entries[0].Index:]
	}

	offset := entries[0].Index - ms.ents[0].Index
	switch {
	case uint64(len(ms.ents)) > offset:
		// NB: full slice expression protects ms.ents at index >= offset from
		// rewrites, as they may still be referenced from outside InMemoryRaftLog.
		ms.ents = append(ms.ents[:offset:offset], entries...)
	case uint64(len(ms.ents)) == offset:
		ms.ents = append(ms.ents, entries...)
	default:
		getLogger().Panicf("missing log entry [last: %d, append at: %d]",
			ms.lastIndex(), entries[0].Index)
	}
	return nil
}
